info:31 Reviews

posted:Posted April 16, 2023
msg:I recently stayed at Nanyuan Hotel during my visit to Ningbo, and I must say, I was impressed. The room was spacious, clean and comfortable, with a lovely bathtub to relax in after a long day of sightseeing. I was also pleasantly surprised to receive a complementary bowl of fruits on arrival, which was a nice touch. The hotel staff were friendly and accommodating, even offering complementary yogurt during my stay.

The breakfast spread was good, although I would have preferred more western food options. Unfortunately, when I visited, they had run out of fried bacon. However, this did not detract from the overall experience. I also appreciated the option of a late check-out, which allowed me to leave after 1 PM.

Overall, I would recommend Nanyuan Hotel to anyone visiting Ningbo. The staff were friendly, the room was comfortable, and the complementary extras were a nice touch. I would definitely consider staying here again, provided the price is right.

Apologies about my photos, I remembered to take them only when I was a bout to check out.

msg:Let's talk about the service first: Front Office: We booked two superior rooms. We arrived at the hotel at around 11:00 am on the 3rd. We asked if we could check in, but we didn't expect to be arranged to check in directly. When checking in, the waiter named Wang Qing on the badge upgraded the room type for our two rooms and checked in very quickly! My parents were very happy, and the rooms were very close. The five-star praise for the service is for her.
However, the room service was a little worse. There was only shampoo but no conditioner (this can be a reminder to other tourists and friends, you have to bring your own conditioner), and other disposable toiletries were in small quantities. You can choose to bring your own or ask the room to deliver, but it took a long time to deliver (after three phone calls to urge, it took about an hour in total). Maybe it was a holiday, so it was busy! Cleaning the next day, the garbage in the trash can was confiscated. They called at 8 o'clock in the morning to ask if we wanted to clean the room! It may not be very friendly to guests who may want to sleep in!
Restaurant: Breakfast is a combination of Chinese and Western food, generally speaking, it's okay! Coffee, bread, wontons, noodles, co**** grains, vegetables, fruits, beverages, milk and yogurt are basically all covered. The waiter was also very diligent and could close the dishes in time when he saw that the dishes were empty.
The hotel is located a little south of the city center, and the location is good. It is basically within three kilometers to the downtown area of ‚Äã‚Äãthe scenic spot, and the taxi will not exceed 15 yuan. It is quite convenient.

In short, the hotel is good, with a magnificent appearance, a good environment, and good room hygiene. I will choose Nanyuan next time I come, and I look forward to the improvement of the service of the housekeeping department
